Core Joda-Beans Domain Classes (modules/product/)\\n\\nThe `FxVanillaOption` type family consists of four core domain classes located in the product module:\\n\\n1. **FxVanillaOption** (`modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOption.java`)\\n   - Class: `FxVanillaOption`\\n   - A Joda-Beans immutable domain class annotated with `@BeanDefinition`\\n   - Implements `FxOptionProduct`, `Resolvable<ResolvedFxVanillaOption>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\\n   - Represents a vanilla FX option with a vanilla payoff structure\\n\\n2. **FxVanillaOptionTrade** (`modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTrade.java`)\\n   - Class: `FxVanillaOptionTrade`\\n   - A Joda-Beans immutable domain class annotated with `@BeanDefinition`\\n   - Implements `FxOptionTrade`, `ResolvableTrade<ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\\n   - Represents an OTC trade in an FxVanillaOption with trade metadata and premium\\n\\n3. **ResolvedFxVanillaOption** (`modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOption.java`)\\n   - Class: `ResolvedFxVanillaOption`\\n   - A Joda-Beans immutable domain class annotated with `@BeanDefinition`\\n   - Implements `ResolvedProduct`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\\n   - The resolved form of FxVanillaOption, bound to reference data (holiday calendars, curves)\\n   - Primary input to the pricers\\n\\n4. **ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade** (`modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade.java`)\\n   - Class: `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade`\\n   - A Joda-Beans immutable domain class annotated with `@BeanDefinition`\\n   - Implements `ResolvedTrade`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\\n   - The resolved form of FxVanillaOptionTrade, primary input to the pricers\\n\\n### 2. Pricer Classes (modules/pricer/)\\n\\nFour pricer classes are available for FxVanillaOption, implementing two pricing methodologies (Black lognormal model and Vanna-Volga method), each with both product and trade variants:\\n\\n1. **BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (`modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java`)\\n   - Class: `BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer`\\n   - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` products using the Black lognormal model\\n   - Uses `BlackFxOptionVolatilities` for volatility inputs\\n\\n2. **BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (`modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java`)\\n   - Class: `BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer`\\n   - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` trades using the Black lognormal model\\n   - Delegates product pricing to `BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer`\\n   - Includes premium pricing via `DiscountingPaymentPricer`\\n   - Provides methods for present value, delta, currency exposure, and implied volatility calculations\\n\\n3. **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer** (`modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer.java`)\\n   - Class: `VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer`\\n   - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` products using the Vanna-Volga method\\n   - Uses `BlackFxOptionSmileVolatilities` for volatility inputs (smile-based term structure)\\n\\n4. **VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer** (`modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/fxopt/VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer.java`)\\n   - Class: `VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer`\\n   - Prices `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` trades using the Vanna-Volga method\\n   - Delegates product pricing to `VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer`\\n   - Includes premium pricing via `DiscountingPaymentPricer`\\n\\n### 3. Measure Calculation Classes (modules/measure/)\\n\\nFour classes in the measure module wire pricers to the calculation engine and support multi-scenario calculations:\\n\\n1. **FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations** (`modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations.java`)\\n   - Class: `FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations`\\n   - Final class (package-private) handling multi-scenario measure calculations\\n   - Composition of both `BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer` and `VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer`\\n   - Used internally by `FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction`\\n\\n2. **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations** (`modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations.java`)\\n   - Class: `FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations`\\n   - Public class providing high-level calculation API for FX vanilla option trades\\n   - Takes `BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer` and `VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer` in constructor\\n   - Exposes methods for present value, sensitivities, and other measures\\n\\n3. **FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction** (`modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction.java`)\\n   - Class: `FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction`\\n   - Implements `CalculationFunction<FxVanillaOptionTrade>`\\n   - Integrates with Strata's calculation framework\\n   - Resolves trades and applies appropriate pricers based on scenario data\\n\\n4. **FxVanillaOptionMethod** (`modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/fxopt/FxVanillaOptionMethod.java`)\\n   - Enum: `FxVanillaOptionMethod`\\n   - Implements `NamedEnum`, `CalculationParameter`\\n   - Defines pricing methods available: `BLACK` and `VANNA_VOLGA`\\n   - Provides the link between market data and pricing methods\\n\\n### 4. Loader/CSV Plugin (modules/loader/)\\n\\n**FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin** (`modules/loader/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/loader/csv/FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin.java`)\\n- Class: `FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin`\\n- Implements `TradeCsvParserPlugin`, `TradeCsvWriterPlugin<FxVanillaOptionTrade>`\\n- Handles CSV parsing and writing for FxVanillaOptionTrade\\n- Supports round-trip serialization of trades\\n- Integrates with Strata's CSV loader framework for trade data persistence\\n\\n### 5. FxSingleBarrierOption - Embedded FxVanillaOption Dependency\\n\\n**FxSingleBarrierOption** (`modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/fxopt/FxSingleBarrierOption.java`)\\n- Class: `FxSingleBarrierOption`\\n- A Joda-Beans immutable domain class annotated with `@BeanDefinition`\\n- Implements `FxOptionProduct`, `Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\\n- **Contains `FxVanillaOption` as the `underlyingOption` field (dependency)**\\n- Represents a barrier option wrapping a vanilla FX option with additional barrier and rebate specifications\\n- Static factory methods: `of(FxVanillaOption underlyingOption, Barrier barrier, CurrencyAmount rebate)` and `of(FxVanillaOption underlyingOption, Barrier barrier)`\\n\\n## Type Family Hierarchy\\n\\nThe type family follows this resolution chain:\\n1. **Trade Level**: `FxVanillaOptionTrade` → `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade`\\n2. **Product Level**: `FxVanillaOption` → `ResolvedFxVanillaOption`\\n3. **Pricing**: Both product and trade levels have Black and Vanna-Volga variant pricers\\n4. **Calculation Framework**: Measurement functions aggregate pricers and integrate with Strata's calculation engine\\n5. **Data Loading**: CSV plugin enables persistence and loading of trades\\n6. **Extension**: `FxSingleBarrierOption` extends the vanilla option with barrier features\\n\\n## Architecture Summary\\n\\nThe complete type family demonstrates OpenGamma Strata's well-structured approach to financial instruments:\\n\\n- **Domain Classes**: Clean separation between unresolved (FxVanillaOption, FxVanillaOptionTrade) and resolved (ResolvedFxVanillaOption, ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade) forms\\n- **Pricing Layer**: Multiple pricing models (Black, Vanna-Volga) with dedicated product and trade pricers\\n- **Measure Calculation**: Integration with the calculation framework via CalculationFunction and multi-scenario support\\n- **Data Persistence**: CSV loader for trade serialization\\n- **Composition**: FxSingleBarrierOption demonstrates composition pattern where barrier options embed vanilla options\\n\\nAll classes are located
